 * Result: It fails. His density isn't high enough yet. The spear breaks his shoulder. He saves Issei, but he goes down.
 * Impact: Rias heals him but still offers the "Memory Wipe" because she sees him as fragile.
 * Ariel's Reaction: He refuses the wipe. But unlike Ren (who gets depressed/envious), Ariel gets Analytical.
   * Ariel: "My density was 40% too low. I need to increase muscle fiber contraction speed."
2. The Gap Week (The Optimization)
 * Action: He dives into the PTD.
 * Method: He doesn't just do pushups. He runs combat simulations against Raynare 100 times a night. He learns her attack patterns. He refines his Observation.
 * Status: He heals fast (Bio-Feedback), but he isn't "God Level" yet. He is "Solid Snake" level.
3. The Church Raid (The Competent Soldier)
 * Ren's Raid (Route B): Dirty, desperate, using sand and sewers.
 * Ariel's Raid (Route A): Tactical Precision.
   * Vs. Freed: Ariel doesn't brawl. He uses CQC to disarm Freed in 3 moves because he simulated Freed's fighting style in the PTD. He wins efficiently, taking minor damage.
   * Vs. Raynare: When she throws the spear, Ariel doesn't just tank it. He Deflects it. He uses a steel pipe reinforced with basic Ki to slap the spear aside.
 * The Result: He survives without major injury. He helps Issei win.
 * Rias's Reaction: "You improved remarkably fast. You have talent."
   * She stops seeing him as a victim and starts seeing him as a Prospect.
âš–ï¸ Why this is better
It makes Ariel's "Legendary Mentor" status earned.
He didn't start strong. He became strong by learning from his failure in Chapter 1. It validates his philosophy: "Data beats Talent."
This preserves the Ariel Archetype (Optimistic Grinder) while removing the "Overpowered Isekai Protagonist" vibe from the start.

***

Pause, how would you make Ariel's full version? The simple question is where do you think Ariel starts to show strenght? Or analyze every events and what if early and what if late?

***

This is a crucial narrative design choice. Ariel is the "Optimistic Grinder" (Goku/Luffy archetype). Unlike Ren, who is defined by the ceiling, Ariel is defined by breaking through.
The question is When does the breakthrough happen?
If he breaks through too early, he steals Isseiâ€™s thunder. If he breaks through too late, he feels incompetent.
Here is the analysis of the three major "Reveal Points" and my recommendation for the Full Version.
1. Event: The Raynare Incident (The Park)
 * What Happens: Raynare attacks Issei.
 * Option A (Early Strength): Ariel stops the spear with Will/Iron Body.
   * Pros: Immediate badass factor. Establishes him as a "Variable" instantly.
   * Cons: Rias treats him as a threat/anomaly immediately. It lowers the stakes for Isseiâ€™s death/resurrection. It removes the "Motivation" for Ariel to train harder (he already won).
 * Option B (Late Strength): Ariel tries to block but gets Broken (Bone fracture).
   * Pros: Trauma. It proves that "Theory (PTD)" is not "Practice." It gives him a personal reason to hate his weakness. It aligns him with Issei as a "victim" who needs to rise up.
 * Verdict: LATE (Failure). Ariel must fail here. It validates the need for the PTD grind.
2. Event: The Church Raid (Asia Rescue)
 * What Happens: The duo raids the church to save Asia.
 * Option A (Early Strength): Ariel uses Flash Step and Ki Blasts to wreck Freed and Raynare.
   * Pros: Very satisfying. Shows rapid growth.
   * Cons: It overshadows Issei unlocking the Boosted Gear. Why does Issei need to be the hero if Ariel can just solo the dungeon?
 * Option B (Balanced/Tactical Strength): Ariel uses CQC (Snake) and Gadgets (Batman).
   * Action: He disarms Freed using technique, not power. He survives Raynare by predicting (Observation) and dodging, not tanking.
   * Pros: It establishes Ariel as the "Skill" to Issei's "Power." It earns Rias's respect ("You are a capable soldier") without terrifying her ("You are a monster").
 * Verdict: MIDDLE (Competence). He shouldn't be "Strong" yet, but he should be "Effective."
3. Event: Riser Phenexâ€™s Arrival (The Fireball)
 * What Happens: Riser burns the clubroom.
 * Option A (The Reveal): Ariel steps in and Punches the Fire.
   * Context: He has spent the "Gap Week" abusing the PTD (Bio-Feedback/Regen) to accelerate his growth.
   * Impact: This is the perfect moment. Riser is an "Unbeatable" enemy. Ariel proving that human physics can stop Devil magic is the paradigm shift.
 * Option B (Wait for Game): Ariel does nothing.
   * Cons: If he waits too long, the Peerage treats him like a mascot for too long. He needs to earn his spot on the Training Camp roster as a "Sensei," not a "Cook."
 * Verdict: EARLY (The Breakout). This is the moment Ariel becomes the Legend.
ðŸš€ The Recommended Progression for Ariel (Full Version)
This curve creates the most satisfying reading experience:
 * Phase 1 (The Failure): Ariel gets broken by Raynare. He realizes his "Human Body" is trash.
 * Phase 2 (The Optimization): During recovery, he uses the PTD to Bio-Hack. He forces his body to heal in 24 hours. He unlocks Logic/Tactics.
 * Phase 3 (The Proof): At the Church, he proves that Intelligence > Magic by dismantling Freed with CQC. He earns his place as an ally.
 * Phase 4 (The Grind): In the gap before Riser, he unlocks Ki/Iron Body.
 * Phase 5 (The Reveal): He stops Riser's fire. The Peerage goes from "He's smart" to "He's strong."
ðŸ“ Summary Comparison
| Event | Ren (Route B) | Ariel (Route A - Full) |
|---|---|---|
| Raynare | Trauma: Breaks arm. Saves Issei physically. Pitied. | Failure: Breaks arm. Saves Issei physically. Analyzes the failure immediately. |
| Church | Dirty: Uses sand/sewers. Sacrifices himself (victim). | Tactical: Uses CQC/Gadgets. Outplays the enemy (soldier). |
| Riser Intro | Silence: Watches coldly. Analyzes weakness. | Defiance: Punches the fire. Proves Human Potential. |
| Camp Role | Cook: Isolated. Trains in secret. | Sensei: Leads training. Shares the PTD wisdom. |
Conclusion:
Ariel's "Full Version" should focus on competence rising to power. He starts as a guy who knows how to fight but lacks the stats, and ends as a guy who has both.

Pause and another extension, Ariel full version is not only Riser arc but whole highschool dxd, will you change your approach and how is the rest of the plan until ending?

***

This is a massive expansion, but a necessary one. If we are running the Full Version (Volumes 1â€“25+), the narrative approach for Ariel must change as the series progresses.
Why? Because High School DxD suffers from extreme power creep.
 * Early Game: Breaking a wall is impressive.
 * Late Game: Destroying a dimension is standard.
If Ariel stays as just a "Tactician with Iron Body," he becomes irrelevant by Volume 5. To keep up with Issei (who becomes a Dragon God), Ariel must evolve from a Soldier into a God.
Here is the Long-Term Roadmap for Ariel Caelum Veritas, mapping his "Library of Legends" progression to the DxD arcs.
ðŸš€ The Evolution Strategy: "From Soldier to God"
The Approach Change:
 * Vols 1-4 (The Mortal): Ariel uses Tactics, CQC, and basic Haki. He fights smarter, not harder. He is the "Sensei."
 * Vols 5-12 (The Super-Human): Ariel hits the biological limit. He shifts focus to Ki Cultivation and Wuxia Body Refinement to survive battles with Gods. He becomes the "Brother/Rival."
 * Vols 12+ (The Divine Aspirant): Ariel taps into Dragon Ball Super / Gosu. He stops trying to be a "Strong Human" and starts trying to be a "Deity."
ðŸ—ºï¸ The Arc-by-Arc Breakdown
1. The Awakening Arcs (Vol 1-2: Raynare & Riser)
 * Status: Solid Snake / Early Sanji.
 * Modules: CQC, Iron Body (Tekkai), Basic Observation.
 * Role: The Tactician.
 * The Climax: Punching Riserâ€™s fire (as discussed). He proves Human Will > Low-Tier Magic.
2. The Holy Sword Arc (Vol 3: Kokabiel)
 * The Threat: Light Speed attacks (Kokabiel).
 * The Upgrade: Observation Haki (Future Sight).
   * Ariel cannot move at light speed yet. He survives by predicting where the light will be.
   * Feat: He intercepts a light spear meant for Rias not by speed, but by already being there.
 * Library: Katakuri (One Piece) + Minato (Naruto - Reflexes).
 * Relationship: He saves Kiba from his vengeance obsession by defeating a Holy Sword user with a wooden stick, proving the weapon doesn't make the warrior.
3. The Peace Summit (Vol 4: Vali Lucifer)
 * The Threat: Vali Lucifer (The White Dragon). A prodigy.
 * The Upgrade: Advanced Armament (Ryou/Internal Destruction).
   * Valiâ€™s armor is too hard to break from the outside. Ariel learns to throw his Ki inside the armor to damage the user.
 * Library: Rayleigh (Internal Destruction) + Mori Jin (Renewal Taekwondo).
 * Interaction: Vali ignores everyone except Issei... and Ariel.
   * Vali: "You have no dragon. Why does your punch hurt?"
   * Ariel: "Because I hit your soul, not your suit."
4. The Underworld Training Arc (Vol 5: Sairaorg)
 * The Event: The Gremory Peerage trains in the Underworld.
 * The Best Friend: Ariel meets Sairaorg Bael.
   * Sairaorg is a Devil with no magic who uses Touki (Physical Ki).
   * Ariel is a Human with no magic who uses Haki.
   * Result: They become Soul Brothers. They spar for days. Sairaorg teaches Ariel how to generate Touki (Life Spirit), massively boosting Ariel's base stats.
 * The Upgrade: Kaioken (Limit Breaking). Ariel learns to multiply his output at the cost of damage.
5. The Hero Faction Arc (Vol 9-12: Cao Cao)
 * The Threat: Cao Cao (True Longinus). A Human who defeats Devils.
 * The Ideological Clash:
   * Cao Cao: "Humans are superior because of Tools (Sacred Gears)."
   * Ariel: "Humans are superior because of Effort."
 * The Upgrade: Conqueror's Haki (Authority).
   * Cao Cao tries to use the Spear's "Truth" ability.
   * Ariel counters with his own "Veritas."
   * Feat: Ariel splits the sky (Roger vs. Whitebeard style) clashing against the True Longinus with his bare fist.
6. The Evil Dragon / Beast Arc (Vol 20+: Trihexa)
 * The Threat: Planetary Destruction.
 * The Upgrade: God Ki / Ultra Instinct (Omen).
   * Ariel finally unlocks the "Dragon Ball Super" tier. He converts his Touki/Haki into Divine Energy.
 * The Feat: While Issei fights the main body of Trihexa (DxD Form), Ariel holds off the legion of mass-produced Evil Dragons alone.
   * Library: Beerus / Whis.
   * He uses Hakai (Destruction) to erase an Evil Dragon from existence.
ðŸŒŒ The Endgame State (The God of Will)
By the end of the series, Ariel is no longer a "Human." He has achieved Apotheosis through martial arts (The Sage/God Tier).
 * Relationship with Rias: She stops being his "King" and becomes his Equal. The romance (if any) is based on mutual respect between two leaders.
 * Relationship with Issei: They are the Red and Blue Oni. Issei is the Dragon of Domination; Ariel is the God of Discipline.
Does this roadmap align with your vision?
It shifts the genre from "School Battle" to "Cosmic Martial Arts Epic" as the series goes on.

Still pause. Since you mentioned High School DxD suffers from extreme power creep I took a quick look. It made me think that both Ren even Ariel have to leave to catch up and only visits few times to fix tragedies and in the end save everyone that suffers from the ending tragedy or do you think otherwise?

***

You are absolutely right. The power creep in High School DxD is exponential. By Volume 10+, characters are throwing around attacks that can wipe out countries. By the end, they are dealing with beings that threaten the planet or dimension.
For a Human (even a superhuman one) to keep up with Dragon Gods and Beasts of Apocalypse, training in a park or a gym isn't enough. They need a Hyperbolic Time Chamber or a magic-rich environment.
Your idea is the most logical solution:
Both Ariel and Ren MUST use the Corridor/Other Worlds to "Grind" in environments that allow them to surpass the DxD logic.
Here is how this "Guardian / Fix-It" dynamic would work for the Full Version:
ðŸŒŒ The "Off-World Grinders" Concept
Instead of being constant party members (who might slow down the plot or get overshadowed), Ariel and Ren become Recurring Guest Stars / Guardians.
1. The Necessity of Departure (The Power Gap)
 * Ariel: Realizes around Volume 4 (Vali Arc) that he can't fight White Dragon Emperors with just "Iron Body." He needs to learn God Ki or Planetary Destruction. Earth doesn't have the mana density for that.
 * Ren: Realizes his "Void" is dangerous to his friends. He needs to go to the Deep Void to master it without hurting anyone.
 * The Agreement: They agree to leave the "Main Quest" (Issei's Harem Adventure) to Issei. They will go on a "Side Quest for Ultimate Power" so they can return to save everyone when the plot gets too dark.
2. The "Visiting" Dynamic (Fixing Tragedies)
They don't disappear forever. They pop back in specifically to Fix Plotholes or Prevent Tragedy.
 * Visit 1: The Holy Sword Arc (Saving Kiba's Soul)
   * Canon: Kiba suffers a breakdown.
   * Fix: Ariel returns from a "Training Trip." He brings a technique to let Kiba speak to the souls of his friends, giving him closure before he goes berserk.
 * Visit 2: The Peace Summit (Stopping the Terrorists)
   * Canon: Vali attacks. Chaos ensues.
   * Fix: Ren steps out of a portal. He uses Void Gravity to pin down the Chaos Brigade magicians, turning a chaotic battle into a controlled duel between Issei and Vali.
 * Visit 3: The Dimensional Gap (Saving Issei)
   * Canon: Issei "dies" and his soul drifts in the Gap.
   * Fix: Ren lives in the Gap. He catches Issei's soul immediately.
   * Ren: "You're early. Grab a chair."
3. The Endgame (Saving the Ending)
This is the big payoff you mentioned.
 * Canon Tragedy: Sirzechs (Rias's brother) and other leaders sacrifice themselves to seal Trihexa (666), leaving Rias heartbroken and the Underworld without leaders.
 * The Fix: Ariel and Ren return at Full Power.
   * Ariel (God of Destruction Mode): Fights Trihexa physically, matching the Beast's strength.
   * Ren (Cosmic Sage Mode): Opens a massive Corridor. Instead of Sirzechs sealing himself, Ren seals Trihexa into a pocket dimension he created.
   * Result: Sirzechs lives. Rias is happy. The "Tragedy" is averted by the two humans who became Gods in the shadows.
âš–ï¸ The Narrative Structure
This approach creates a very satisfying Dual Narrative:
 * The Main Story (Issei): We follow Issei dealing with school, girls, and growing up.
 * The Interludes (Ariel/Ren): Every few chapters, we get a glimpse of Ariel and Ren in some hellish dimension, fighting Eldritch horrors or training with Alien Masters, getting impossibly strong off-screen.
 * The Crossovers: When they meet, Issei is shocked by how much stronger they are, and they are charmed by how "grounded" Issei still is.
Conclusion:
Yes. Leaving to Catch Up is the best writing decision.
 * It explains their power growth.
 * It keeps them mysterious and cool.
 * It allows them to be the "Deus Ex Machina" that fixes the sad parts of the original story.
Shall we resume the Ren Demo (Day 36/37) with the understanding that his departure is leading toward this "Guardian" future?

ðŸŒŒ Why this is the Best Approach

   * We see Ariel struggle alone (Route A).
   * When they finally meet in Route D/E (NG+), the satisfaction of seeing them work together is earned because we know how hard it was for them individually.

   * By having them be "Regression" characters (Retaining memories/techniques but resetting bodies), you solve the problem of them being weak humans. They know the shortcuts. They know about Ki, Haki, and the Void from Day 1.

   * Knowing the plot allows them to save people who died or suffered (Kiba's friends, Asia, Koneko's trauma) efficiently.
   * It changes the genre from Survival Horror (Ren's Demo) to Strategic Domination (NG+).

This creates a grounded, relatable dynamic for the NG+. They aren't ancient gods pretending to be human; they are tired veterans trying to relive their high school days correctly.
Here is the breakdown for the New Game+ Setup.
1. Ariel's Role: The "Straight Man" (The Anchor)
If Ren is the "Dark Member" of the Perverted Quartet, Ariel needs to be the Social Camouflage.
 * Role: The "Normal Guy" / Unofficial Class Rep.
 * Dynamic: He hangs out with the Quartet, but he is the one who says, "Guys, maybe we shouldn't peep today, we have a test."
 * Function: This allows Ariel to interact with Sona Sitri and Rias socially without being dismissed as "just another pervert." He is the bridge between the "Losers" (The Quartet) and the "Elites" (The Devils).
2. Ren's Perversion: The "Roleplay"
You are spot on. Since Ren spent ~1 year in the Void/Isolation, his hormonal drive is dampened by discipline and trauma. He isn't "horny" anymore; he is Tired.
 * The Act: He plays the role of the "Strategist Pervert" because he knows it makes Issei happy. It maintains the bond of the Quartet.
 * The Internal Monologue: "I have stared into the abyss of non-existence. Peeping on the Kendo club seems... trivial. But Issei is smiling, so I will calculate the viewing angle."
 * The Request: Ren definitely asks Ariel for help.
   * Ren: "Ariel. They want to raid the girls' locker room again. I can't do this alone. I'll die of cringe. Please come and be the 'Lookout' so we don't actually get caught."
   * Ariel: (Sighing) "Fine. But I'm bringing a book. And if Koneko shows up, I'm selling you out."
3. The Power Scale: "Veterans," not "Sages"
Since only "a little time" (approx. 1 Year Subjective) has passed for both since their Demos:
 * They are NOT Gods. They can't snap their fingers and erase the universe.
 * They ARE Pro-Gamers. They know the mechanics. They know the shortcuts.
 * The Struggle: Their minds are Level 50, but their bodies are Level 1.
   * Ren: Knows how to open the Corridor, but his body isn't tough enough to survive inside for long.
   * Ariel: Knows how to use Haki, but his bones aren't dense enough to punch Riser without breaking.
ðŸŽ­ Sample Interaction: NG+ Day 1
Location: The Street Corner (The Fist Bump).
Ren: "So. Back to square one."
Ariel: "We kept the memories. That's enough."
Ren: "I have to go meet Matsuda and Motohama. We have a 'Summer Magazine' council." (Ren looks exhausted). "Ariel. Please. Join the group. I can't handle their energy alone. I need a sane person to talk to."
Ariel: (Laughing) "You want me to join the Perverted Quartet? I'm the respectable one."
Ren: "You're the one who wants to punch a God of Destruction. You're crazier than they are. Just... be the lookout. Keep me sane."
Ariel: "Fine. Sworn brothers, right? I'll watch your back while you watch... magazines."

This interaction creates a hilarious "Chaos Engine" within the group.
In the previous versions (Ren & Ariel only), the dynamic was "One works, One watches."
With Kala, the dynamic becomes "Two try to control the situation, One pours gasoline on the fire."
Here is how the Perverted Quartet + The Veritas Siblings operates during a scheme.
ðŸŽ­ The New Dynamic: The Architect, The Guard, and The Muse
1. Ren (The Reluctant Architect)
 * Role: He still plans the schemes because the Trio is incompetent without him. He treats it like a military operation to ensure nobody gets caught (damage control).
 * Attitude: "I am doing this so you don't get expelled. Please be quiet."
2. Ariel (The Enforcing Guard)
 * Role: He refuses to peep, but he refuses to let Ren go to jail. He stands guard at the perimeter with his arms crossed, radiating "Don't mess with us" energy.
 * Attitude: "I will give you ten minutes. If Koneko comes, I am whistling once. If you don't run, you die."
3. Kala (The Chaotic Consultant)
 * Role: She finds the boys' desperation adorable and hilarious. She doesn't stop them; she Critiques them.
 * Attitude: "Peeping through a hole? That's so low-effort! If you want to see girls, you have to be smarter! Make them want to show you!"
ðŸŽ¬ Scenario: The "Pool Cleaning" Scheme
Context: The Trio wants to see the Swim Team. They plan to drill a hole in the changing room wall.
The Planning Session (Clubroom/Classroom):
Matsuda: "The drill is ready! We go in at 0400!"
Motohama: "For the dream!"
Ren: (Rubbing his temples) "Drilling is too loud. The acoustics in the locker room will amplify the vibration. You'll be caught in 12 seconds."
Ariel: (Reading a book by the door) "And Sona has motion sensors on the perimeter now. I saw Tsubaki installing them."
Issei: "Damn! We're doomed!"
Kala: (Pops up from behind Ren, stealing his chips) "Why don't you just volunteer?"
The Trio: "Goddess Kala?!"
Kala: "Drilling is for criminals. But the Swim Team needs the pool cleaned before the season starts, right? If you volunteer to scrub the pool..."
She winks.
"...you're legally inside the splash zone."
Issei: "GENIUS! KALA-SENPAI IS A GENIUS!"
Ren: (Looking at Ariel) "She's enabling them."
Ariel: (Sighing) "It's better than property damage. I guess we're cleaning the pool."
âš”ï¸ The Execution: The Veritas Shift
At the Pool:
The boys are scrubbing the floor. The Swim Team girls arrive.
1. The Trio (Issei/Matsuda/Motohama):
They are drooling, trying to look cool while holding mops. They are obviously perverted.
 * Girl A: "Ugh, the Beast Trio is looking at us."
2. Ren (The Worker):
He is scrubbing the tiles with Void-Enhanced Speed. He isn't looking at the girls; he's looking at the grime. He wants to finish the job so he can go home.
 * Girl B: "Hey, the quiet one... he's actually working really hard. He looks kinda cool."
3. Ariel (The Lifeguard):
Ariel is standing by the deep end, "Supervising." He is shirtless (showing off his 2.0 PHY physique). He isn't looking at the girls; he's scanning for stray magic/threats.
 * Girl C: "Is that Ariel-kun? Look at those abs... forget the swim team, look at him!"
4. Kala (The Distraction):
Kala shows up in a swimsuit (because she does what she wants).
 * The Result: Chaos.
   * The Trio faints from nosebleeds.
   * The Swim Team girls are jealous/intimidated by her perfect proportions.
   * Issei is crying tears of joy.
Ren: (To Ariel) "We failed. The mission was 'See Girls.' The result is 'Issei is unconscious and Kala is starting a beach volleyball tournament'."
Ariel: "Mission abort. Grab Issei's legs. I'll grab the shoulders. We're leaving."
Kala: (Waving) "Bye-bye! Don't forget to buy ice cream on the way home!"
ðŸ§  How this affects the Brotherhood
This dynamic creates a specific loop that strengthens their bond:
 * Shared Burden: Ariel and Ren bond over the exhaustion of managing the chaos.
   * Ren: "Why did we agree to this?"
   * Ariel: "Because if we didn't, Kala would have given them a teleportation scroll and sent them into the women's bath."
   * Ren: "Fair point."
 * Kala as the Bridge: Kala prevents Ren from becoming too cynical ("Perverts are trash") and prevents Ariel from being too strict ("Training is everything"). She forces them to engage in Silly Teenage Stuff, which grounds them.
 * The Harem Aspect:
   * Since Kala is the "Unattainable Goddess" to the Trio, Issei stops seeing Ren/Ariel as competition and starts seeing them as Gatekeepers.
   * Issei: "Ren! Ariel! Please put in a good word for me with your sister!"
   * Ren/Ariel: (In unison) "No."
This is the healthiest version of the group. They are a dysfunctional family unit protecting the protagonist from his own stupidity.

Ariel sets up a barbell (or a car).

Vali and Ariel are shirtless, sweating, screaming.

ðŸ’¡ Why this works

 * Sona cares about Rules. Ren cares about Efficiency.

 * Vali cares about Magic Power. Ariel cares about Gains.
They "Break" the genre by refusing to play by its standard rules (Magic/Lineage), forcing the DxD cast to interact with them on human terms.

ðŸ  Scene 1: The Midnight Kitchen (Heartwarming/Quiet)

Here is the Ultimate Epilogue Blueprint for the NG+ Route.
ðŸŒŒ The Grand Finale: The Verdict of the Architect
Timeline: Post-Trihexa Victory (End of Series).
Location: The Dimensional Gap (The Great Red's Domain).
1. The Stage is Set
The war is over. Trihexa is defeated (sealed by Ren, beaten by Ariel). Issei is the Dragon God.
The Veritas Siblings (Ariel, Ren, Kala) stand on a floating island in the Void. The Gremory Peerage and the Leaders (Sirzechs, Azazel, Michael) are present.
Kala: "Well! That was fun! We broke the script, fixed the trauma, and saved the cat!"
Ariel: "We optimized the timeline. Casualty rate: 0%."
Ren: "We survived. That's enough."
Suddenly, the Void goes silent. Even Great Red stops swimming.
A Golden Rift opens. It is not Magic. It is not Haki. It is Source Code.
Kala: (Smiling) "He's here. Everyone, best behavior! The Boss is logging in."
2. The Descent of Kairos
A figure descends. He doesn't look like a warrior or a mage. He looks like a Scholar or an Observer. He wears robes that shift between the textures of the universe (Starfield, Matrix Code, Ink).
Kairos Draco Veritas.
Sirzechs: "Who is... that?"
Azazel: "I don't know. But my Sacred Gear research just became obsolete. That being is the System."
Kairos lands. He looks at the Veritas Siblings.
Kairos: "Mission Complete. Protocol: Veritas."
3. The First Revelation: The Original Canon
Kairos raises a hand. A massive screen appears in the sky.
Kairos: "Behold. The path you were spared."
The screen plays the Original High School DxD Canon.
 * Issei dying alone in the park.
 * Asia dying in the church.
 * Kiba suffering from the Holy Sword trauma.
 * Koneko's fear. Akeno's self-hatred. Rias's despair at the wedding.
 * The death of Sirzechs in the Trihexa war.
Rias: "That... that is us. But... broken."
Issei: "We suffered so much."
Kairos: "That was the baseline. A world of pain and triumph, but heavy with loss."
4. The Second Revelation: The Dark Demo (Ren's Burden)
The screen shifts. It turns dark violet.
It shows Ren Nocturnus (Route B).
 * Ren breaking his arms. Ren being ignored. Ren rotting Riser's face.
 * Ren opening the Corridor and leaving Issei behind.
 * The message: "Everyone is a Person, not a Piece."
Issei: (Crying) "Ren... you went through that? You left me?"
Ren: (NG+ Ren puts a hand on Issei's shoulder) "In another life, I did. Because I felt small. But not this time."
5. The Third Revelation: The Light Demo (Ariel's Grind)
The screen shifts. It turns bright gold.
It shows Ariel Caelum (Route A).
 * Ariel screaming in the PTD. Ariel punching fire. Ariel refusing the Evil Piece.
 * The message: "Potential is Limitless."
Kiba: "He fought without magic. He proved we could be better."
Ariel: (NG+ Ariel nods) "And you became better. You surpassed the simulation."
6. The Verdict
Kairos closes the screens. He looks at the assembled cast.
Kairos: "You have witnessed the shadows of what could have been. You have lived the Golden Route. Why?"
He points to the Veritas Siblings.
Kairos: "Because they chose to carry the weight. Ren carried the Darkness so you could stay pure. Ariel carried the Burden so you could fly. Kala carried the Joy so you wouldn't despair."
He turns to the Gremory Peerage.
Kairos: "You are no longer bound by Fate. You are Free."
7. The Departure of the Avatars
Kala claps. "Okay! Wrap it up! Drac-chan has spoken!"
Ariel: "So... is this it? We go back?"
Ren: "The mission is done."
Kairos smiles. It is a human smile.
Kairos: "Not yet. The universe is vast. There are other stories. Other tragedies to fix."
He opens a Prismatic Gate.
Kairos: "Will you join me? Or will you stay?"
The Choice:
The Veritas Siblings look at the Gremory Peerage.
Issei: "You guys are leaving?"
Ren: "We have to, Issei. We're the Fixers. You're the Heroes. You don't need us anymore."
Ariel: "Train hard, Red Dragon. Don't let your form slip."
Kala: "And keep the harem happy!"
They step onto the platform with Kairos.
As they ascend, Issei yells.
Issei: "THANK YOU! FOR EVERYTHING!"
Kairos: (Voice echoing across the dimension) "May the Truth be your guide."
The Gate closes. The Veritas Siblings vanish into the next narrative.
The Gremory Peerage stands in a perfect world, ready to live their lives, knowing the cost of their happiness was paid in full.
